        <div class="comment-text long">
<div class="comment-text-content">As always, great tutorial!

I wanted to mention another git service; Bitbucket.org. It works the same way as Github, same commands and everything. Well, it does use git so all git services will be exactly the same, that's the great thing about git.

One Difference though, BitBucket.org allows private repositories on the free account level. Sometimes a project just isn't ready for public view. You can still share it with others by email and then when ready flip a switch and make it public.﻿</div>    <div class="comment-text-toggle hid">
